<Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
This quaint little market is in an unknown area of Oakland. They have an excellent and diverse selection of pastries, produce, beverages, deli, packaged goods and pretty much anything you could need. The prices are high, but the location is a bit obscure so it is kind of a funny little place. Parking is super easy, they have a lot of spaces right outside. They also have four tables to sit out should you choose to sit outside and enjoy something you purchased.</text>

Smog Hut makes getting a smog quick and enjoyable. Yes, you heard that right, enjoyable. Preet and his teammate are an amazing duo and they are the best at getting the job done efficiently.

< Review>
Linda Betsekas of Print Services won my great respect in recent days as I twice observed her working efficiently on job orders all under the pressure of the watchful eyes of a handful of customers in the que. But impotantly she acknowledged each waiting patron promptly with a smile and then they did not seem to mind the short wait to be served. My jobs amounted to printing out $1.32 worth of return mailing labels. The process was enough to confuse me thoroughly, but in a few minutes Linda had my requests printed-out. Soon I was a happy camper back in the traffic. She treated me as if I had brought in a $500 undertaking. So thank you Linda. Our last names are noticeably similar, but Linda's is Greek and mine is Lithuanian!!!

Jeff Brekas,
Salem-Silverton, Oregon<//Review>
